( - , ) (The Hon. Jeyaraj Fernandopulle - Minister of Highways and Road Development and Chief Government Whip) , . . . Question ordered to stand down. , / : / WALASMULLA DIVISIONAL SECRETARYS DIVISION : GAMA NEGUMA/GEMI ISURA 1375/07 4.

( ) (The Hon. Vijitha Ranaweera) , , , - (2) () (i) 2007 / , (ii) , , (iii) , , ? () (i) . (ii) , (iii) , , ; (ii) ; ? () (i) / ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () / ? () , ?

1909 1910

, , : () (i) 2007 / , (ii) , (iii) , ? () (i) , (ii) / , (iii) , , , (iv) ? () (i) / , (ii) , (iii) ? () / ? () , ?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administration and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Security, Law and Order: (a) Will he inform this House, (i) the amount of money that has been allocated under the Gama Neguma / Gemi Isura programme, to the Walasmulla Divisional Secretariat Division for the year 2007; (ii) if the relevant Divisional Secretariat Division has received the aforesaid amount of money, the date of receipt; and (iii) if not, the date on which the aforesaid amount of money will be received? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, in each of the projects, (i) the development activities that are intended to be carried out using the aforesaid monies;

(ii) the name of the Grama Niladhari Division / village in which those activities will be carried out; (iii) the estimated amount, the date of commencement, the date on which it is expected to be completed; and (iv) the amount of money that has been released for the proposals on which the work has already been commenced? (c) Will he inform this House, (i) the activities for which the involvement of the councilors / members of local government bodies is obtained in implementing these projects; (ii) the criteria on which they are selected; and (iii) their names? (d) Will he inform this House as to how the involvement of the relevant councilors / members is considered legal under the laws pertaining to the subject of Local Government and Provincial Councils? (e) If not, why?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administration and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Security, Law and Order : (a) Will he inform this House, (i) the amount of money that has been allocated under the Gama Neguma / Gemi Isura programme, to the Okewela Divisional Secretarys Division for the year 2007;

2008 04 1919 1920

(ii) if the relevant Divisional Secretarys Division has received the aforesaid amount of money, the date of receipt; and (iii) if not, the date on which the aforesaid amount of money will be received? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, in each of the projects, (i) the development activities that are intended to be carried out using the aforesaid monies; (ii) the name of the Grama Niladhari Division / village in which those activities will be carried out; (iii) the estimated amount, the date of commencement, the date on which it is expected to be completed; and (iv) the amount of money that has been released for the proposals on which the work has already been commenced? ( ) , ? asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administration, and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Security, Law and Order,- (a) Will he inform this House

(i) the amount of money that has been allocated under the Gama Neguma / Gemi Isura programme, to the Beliatta Divisional Secretariat Division for the year 2007;

(ii) if the relevant Divisional Secretarys Division has received the aforesaid amount of money, the date of receipt; and

(iii) if not, the date on which the aforesaid amount of money will be received?

(b) Will he submit to this House, separately in each of the Project

(i) the development activities that are intended to be carried out using the aforesaid monies;

(ii) the name of the Grama Niladhari Division / village in which those activities will be carried out;

(iii) the estimated amount, the date of commencement, the date on which it is expected to be completed; and

(iv) the amount of money that has been released for the proposals on which the work has already been commenced?

(c) Will he inform this House

(i) the activities for which the involvement of the councilors / members of local government bodies is obtained in implementing these projects;

(ii) the criteria on which they are selected; and (iii) their names?

(d) Will he inform this House as to how the involvement of the relevant councilors/ members is considered legal under the laws pertaining to the subject of Local Government and Provincial Councils?

(e) if not, why?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administration and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Security, Law and Order; (a) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of Samurdhi recipients as at 30th June of every year from 2004 to 2007 in the Maharagama Electorate in Colombo District; and (ii) the categories of the above families according to the amount they received? asked the Minister of Irrigation and Water Management and Minister of Ports and Aviation : (a) Is he aware that, (i) Nuwara Wewa in Anuradhapura is a large tank which was built by King Pandukabhaya as far back as 300 A.D.; and (ii) water is supplied to a large number of paddy fields as well as the City of Anuradhapura, from this beautiful tank? (b) Will he inform this House as to on whose order a section of such a national heritage is being filled to build an airstrip? (d) Will he state the reasons for not finding an alternative land for this airstrip? (e) If not, why?

() , ? asked the Minister of Public Administration and Home Affairs,

(a) Is he aware that, (i) Mrs. J.B. Bandaramenika, a Grade II Officer of the Public Management Assistant Service, is presently attached to the office of the Samurdhi Commissioner Generals Department in the Galgamuwa Divisional Secretariat; and

(ii) the Samurdhi Commissioner General in his letter, bearing no: 03/ku-28 and dated 12.04.2007, has intimated to her that her service will be suspended until the approval of the Director of Combined Services is received in terms of Public Administration Circular 30/96, in order to extend her service beyond 55 years? (b) Will he admit the fact that the approval of the Director of Combined Services is not required to extend the services of officers in the Public

1989 1990

[ . ]

Management Service beyond the age of 55 years whereas the aforesaid approval is required to extend the service beyond the age of 57 years? (c) Will he, therefore take steps to make necessary arrangements to allow Mrs. Bandaramenika to serve in her post further since the approval of the Director of Combined Services is not required until she is 57 years old? (d) If not, why?

32(1) , , . 38 , . , , . . ( ) (The Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe) , . , 2001 24 . . They are matters of legislative policy within the purview of Parliament. : The four matters referred taken together, in our view support the inference that the amendment does not remove the executive power of the President in relation to the subjects coming within the purview of the Bill. Although, there is a restriction in the exercise of the discretion hitherto vested in the President, this restriction per se would not be an erosion of the executive power by the President, so as to be inconsistent with Article 3 read with Article 4 (b) of the Constitution." - - . . , , . , . , 2005 15 . 2005 17 "" . . : " ." , 2006 , . . 2007 . , . , - , - . . . .

( ) (The Hon. Jeyaraj Fernandopulle) , . . . . ( ) (The Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe) , . . , ? They are matters of legislative policy within the purview of Parliament. , , ? . . . . . . , . . , , , . . . . . , , - [ ] , . . . . . , , . . , , ? . 2005 17 "" . . . . " ." 2006 . , . . . ( ) (The Hon. Lakshman Senewiratne) . ( ) (The Hon. Jeyaraj Fernandopulle) , . . , .

1993 1994

( ) (The Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe) . , . , . . . , . . ( ) (The Hon. Anura Dissanayake) . , , . [ ]

( ) (The Hon. Jeyaraj Fernandopulle) , . . . ( ) (The Hon. Anura Dissanayake) . , , . , , . , , . . , . . . . . , . . . . , , , . , . , . , . . , . . . , . , , , , ; . ?

, . . , , , , , , . , . . , , , . , , '' '' . . , , . . . , , . . ? 2004 ? 2005 , , , ? , ? ? , . . . . , , . . . , . , , . ( ) (Mr. Speaker) . . . . . ( . . ) (The Hon. K. N. Choksy)

Sir, in regard to the Constitutional Council, I decide to point out that in terms of Article 41A of the Constitution, the Constitutional Council is a permanent body. It is like a Cabinet of Ministers. The Constitution recognizes it

2008 04 1995 1996

and has made a provision for it as a permanent body. For example, the Speaker is an ex officio Member of the Constitutional Council. Even after the dissolution of Parliament, you continue, Mr. Speaker, to be a Member of the Council until the next Parliament is elected and a new Speaker is in place. That clearly indicates that the Constitutional Council is a permanent body. It is not a body that functions at the pleasure of the President. It is a body that is established by the Constitution and there is an obligation, a constitutional duty on the President to appoint a Constitutional Council. Now, he has failed to do so and that failure is a serious violation and an inroad into a Constitutional provision. So, there is no reason why His Excellency the President has not appointed a Constitutional Council. He has not been able to state a reason why and there can be no reason why.

So, it is best in the interest of the country and in the interest of this House, rather than going on with this matter each time the House meets, that the President now makes his position clear and the best he can do is to follow the mandate of the Constitution and put the Constitutional Council in place straightaway. It will be an important body, as important as a Cabinet of Ministers. Therefore, the Constitution cannot function smoothly and continuously without the appointment of this body.

So, I urge the President, in the interest of this House, in the interest of the country and in the interest of his duty of upholding the Constitution, to appoint this Council without further delay.

I thank you.

( ) (The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake)

Hon. Speaker, as a Member of Parliament, I think it is incumbent at least to get an answer to this because we are talking of the Constitution. A breach of the Constitution means, even the Parliament becomes inoperable. So, on that score, Hon. Speaker, I think it is incumbent on you to get from the Leader of the House or the Chief Government Whip, who answers everything, at least an assurance as to when the Prime Minister will give an answer to this particular matter. Various matters which are not important to Parliament are answered within a couple of seconds. But a matter which is very integral to us is not answered. You must put aside your stony silence and ensure that we get a very strong answer to this matter, Hon. Speaker.

( ) (Mr. Speaker) , .

LEAVE OF ABSENCE : HON. ANURA BANDARANAIKE ( ) ( - ) (The Hon. Lasantha Alagiyawanna - Minister of Road Passenger Transport) , : " 66 () , , 2008 04 ." , . . Question put, and agreed to.

( ) (Mr. Speaker) , .

: 2008 26

: 2008 26 PRIVILEGE : DAILY NEWS REPORT OF 26TH FEBRUARY 2008 ( ) (The Hon. John Amaratunga)

Mr. Speaker, I refer to the "Daily News" article titled, ICES imbroglio before NGO Committee appearing on page three of its issue of 26th February, 2008. As you are aware, it is a breach of Privilege of Parliament inasmuch as it is a complete misinterpretation of the proceedings of the said Committee and punishable in terms of Item 5 of Part A of the Schedule to the Parliament (Powers and Privileges) Act and further as the publication of any proceedings in committee of Parliament before they are reported to Parliament is prohibited by Item 9 of Part B of the Schedule to the Parliament (Powers and Privileges) Act, read with Section 22(1) and (2). Furthermore, Article 14 of the Constitution ensures freedom of expression and assembly. Therefore, the people in this country should be free to speak in favour of R2P. The R2P is based on Articles 138 and 139 of the Responsibility to Protect document issued at the High Level Plenary Meeting of the General Assembly of the UN in September, 2005. The Sri Lankan Government was represented by none other than President Kumaratunga who also became a party to it. The report in question falsely makes out that Parliament and the Committee thereof is attempting to stifle the freedom of expression guaranteed to the citizens by our Constitution by summoning and questioning persons who have merely expressed their opinions regarding a matter of public interest. Therefore, I request you to take notice of this breach of Privilege and take such action as appropriate in the circumstances.

Sir, this involves three major issues. One is the publication of Committee proceedings before they are tabled in Parliament as covered by the Parliament (Powers and Privileges) Act. Two, reporting Committee proceedings in which no such decision was taken as reported in the newspapers. The Committee did not take

2005 2006

[ ]

any such decision. Three, giving the impression that the Committee is trying to interfere with the freedom of speech guaranteed in Article 14 of the Constitution. Anyone can make a comment on the Right to Protection or any other matter of public interest. Those people have merely made a comment in terms of Article 14 of the Constitution and are entitled to do so. Sir, it is a very important issue. I would request you to take this matter up before the Committee on Privileges and make a decision on it. Thank you. ( ) (Mr. Speaker) , . . . . ( ) (The Hon. Anura Dissanayake) , . 19 , . 14 , . . 19 , . . , 19 . , , . . , 19 . . 19 . , , - ( ) ( - , ) (The Hon. Piyasena Gamage - Minister of Vocational and Technical Training) 2006 05 . 2007 19 16 . .

WRITTEN ANSWERS TO QUESTIONS :

:

ROAD PASSENGER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY OF UVA PROVINCE : LIEENCES FOR PASSENGER TRANSPORT SERVICES 0796/'06 1.

( ) (The Hon. Vijitha Herath) ,(5) :

2053 2054

() ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () (i) ; (ii) , ; (iii) ; (iv) ; (v) ; ? () , ? , : () , ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , , (ii) , (iii) ?

() (i) , (ii) , , (iii) , (iv) , (v) ?

() , ? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils,(5) (a) Will he inform this House in detail, the procedure followed by the Road Passenger Transport Authority of Uva Province when issuing licenses for buses for passenger transport services? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, the number of passenger transport service licenses issued by the said Authority since the year 2000 up to now along with the names of the licensees, their addresses, the registered numbers of those buses, the relevant routes, the dates of application for license and the dates on which licenses were issued? (c) Will he state separately, (i) if routes have been revised out of those the names of the licensees concerned, their addresses and the registered numbers of the buses; (ii) the former routes and the revised routes; and, (iii) the dates of application for revision and the dates revisions were issued? (d) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of those who have applied for route revisions but not granted so far; (ii) their names, addresses and the dates of application for licenses; (iii) the reasons for not granting the said revisions; (iv) whether approval will be granted for those in future; and, (v) for which licenses? (e) If not, why?

[ ]

2008 04 2055 2056

( )

( - , ) (The Hon. Janaka Bandara Thennakoon - Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils) () . * . * * * , . * . i. ii. iii. iv. v. () . 01 . () i. 02 . ii. 02 . iii. 02 . () i. ii. . iii. . iv. . v. . iv. . () . ( )

( ) .

(a) Yes.

* Obtaining an application form

* Registration

* Obtaining a report from checkers of the Road Passenger Transport Authority regarding the issue of a passenger Transport licence.

* If the request is for other grade roads except A and B grade roades, a report should be obtained from the checker whether the proposed bus is in roadworthy condition.

* Accordingly, in comparison of requests made by the voluntary organizations and passengers the request together with the following certificates are forwarded to the approval of the Chairman of the Provincial Passenger Transport Authority and Passenger Transport licence is issued on receipt of his approval. (i) Fitness certificate of the bus. (ii) Unlimited Insurance certificate. (iii) Revenue licence for the respective year. (iv) Registration certificate of the vehicle. (v) Medical certificate of the driver. (b) Yes. Tabled by Annex -(01) (c) (i) Tabled by Annex-(02) (ii) Tabled by Annex-(02) (iii) Tabled by Annex-(02) (d) There are no licensees who have applied for route revisions and not granted (i) not applicable. (ii) not applicable. (iii) not applicable. (iv) not applicable. (v) not applicable. (vi) not applicable. (e) Not applicable.

ROAD PASSENGER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY OF SA-BARAGAMUWA PROVINCE : LICENCES FOR PASSENGER TRANSPORT SERVICES 0797/'06 2.

( ) (The Hon. Vijitha Herath) -(5) : () ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ?

() (i) ; (ii) , ; (iii) ; (iv) ; (v) ; ? () , ? , : () , ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , , (ii) ,

2008 04 2099 2100

(iii) ? () (i) , (ii) , , (iii) , (iv) , (v) ? () , ? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provin-cial Councils,(5) (a) Will he inform this House in detail, the procedure followed by the Road Passenger Transport Author-ity of Sabaragamuwa when issuing licences for buses for passenger transport services? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, the num-ber of passenger transport service licences issued by the said Authority since the year 2000 up to now along with the names of the licensees, their addresses, the registered numbers of those buses, the relevant routes, the dates of application for licence and the dates on which licences were is-sued? (c) Will he state separately, (i) if routes have been revised out of those the names of the licensees concerned, their ad-dresses and the registered numbers of the buses; (ii) the former routes and the revised routes; and, (iii) the dates of application for revision and the dates revisions were issued? (d) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of those who have applied for route revisions but not granted so far; (ii) their names, addresses and the dates of applica-tion for licences; (iii) the reasons for not granting the said revisions; (iv) whether approval will be granted for those in future; and, (v) for which licences? (e) If not, why?

( ) (The Hon. Janaka Bandara Thennakoon) () . , , . () . 2000 968. ( 01 .) () (i) . (ii) . (iii) . () (i) 32. (ii) 02 . (iii) ? ? . . (iv) . (v) () . () , ? , , . () 2000 968 . ( . 01 .) () (i) .

(ii)

(iii)

2101 2102

[ ] () (i) 32 .

(ii) . 02 .

(iii) ? ? ? . .

(iv) . (v) () (a) Yes, when a passenger transport licence is re-quested from this Authority by a bus owner, firstly the running timetable is checked to find whether times could be allocated for a new bus to run in the requested route and whether it could raise an issue for buses already running in the route. Secondly the request is referred to the Board of Directors. Then a decision will be made whether a passenger trans-port licence is issued or not issued.

(b) Yes, the Authority above has provided 968 passen-ger transport licences since 2000. (Other details have been tabled by Annex 01) (c) (i) Route revisions have not been made. (ii) Not applicable as per above. (iii) Not applicable as per above. (d) (i) The number of those who have applied for route revisions but not granted so far is 32. (ii) tabled by Annex-02. (iii) Action has already been taken to look into whether in the routes for which revisions have been requested the number of buses running is adequate and whether routes requested are suit-able for running buses. After receiving this report. It will take necessary action to issue passenger transport licences with regard to suit-able routes. (iv) If any shortfall arises in the routes of required revisions, the approval would be granted in future. (v) For the passenger transport licences seeking route revisions. (e) Not applicable.

ROAD PASSENGER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY OF NORTH WESTERN PROVINCE : LICENCES FOR PASSENGER TRANSPORT SERVICES 0798/'06 3.

( ) (The Hon. Vijitha Herath) (5) : () ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () (i) ; (ii) , ; (iii) ; (iv) ; (v) ; ? () , ? , : () , ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ,

(ii) , (iii) ? () (i) , (ii) , , (iii) , (iv) , (v) ? () , ? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils : (a) Will he inform this House in detail, the procedure followed by the Road Passenger Transport Authority of North Western Province when issuing licences for buses for passenger transport services? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, the number of passenger transport service licences issued by the said Authority since the year 2000 up to now along with the names of the licensees, their addresses, the registered numbers of those buses, the relevant routes, the dates of application for licence and the dates on which licences were issued? (c) Will he state separately, (i) if routes have been revised out of those the names of the licensees concerned, their addresses and the registered numbers of the buses; (ii) the former routes and the revised routes; and, (iii) the dates of application for revision and the dates revisions were issued? (d) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of those who have applied for route revisions but not granted so far; (ii) their names, addresses and the dates of application for licences; (iii) the reasons for not granting the said revisions; (iv) whether approval will be granted for those in future; and, (v) for which licences? (e) If not, why?

2245 2246

( ) (The Hon. Janaka Bandara Thennakoon) () . . i. . ii. . iii. () / . iv. . v. . () . 890. ( 01 .) () (i) 02 . (ii) 02 . (iii) 02 . () (i) . (ii) . (iii) . (iv) . (v) . () .

() ? . (i) . (ii) . (iii) , , () / . (iv) .

(v) . () 890 ( . 01 .)

() (i) . 02 . (ii) . 02 . (iii) . 02 . () (i) (ii) (iii) (iv) (v)

()

(a) Yes, when an application for passenger transport licence is received, the Authority will take the following action to check whether there is such requirement on the part of passengers. (i) A report on requirements of passengers in the respective route will be obtained from the Divisional Secretary.

(ii) A report of the officers of special operation unit engaged by the Authority for road inspections will also be obtained.

(iii) If it appears that the requirement of buses in that particular route is necessary in terms of such inspections and recommendations, a report will be prepared by the Deputy General Manager (Transport) and submitted to the Board of Directors through General Manager/Secretary to the Board of Directors. (iv) When it is approved by the Board of Directors necessary action will be taken to issue licences. (v) All the applications forwarded to peoples representatives are referred to the Authority and the aforesaid procedure is followed in respect of such applications. (b) Yes. Number of licences is 890 (other details have been tabled by Annex-01). (c) (i) tabled by Annex-02. (ii) tabled by Annex-02. (iii) tabled by Annex-02. (d) (i) When an application is rejected a file will not be maintained. (ii) Not applicable. (iii) arising from issues in regard to transport in the route. (iv) Not applicable. (v) Not applicable. (e) Not applicable.

: : ROAD PASSENGER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY OF SOUTH-ERN PROVINCE : LICENCES FOR PASSENGER TRANSPORT SERVICES 0799/'06 4.

( ) (The Hon. Vijitha Herath) (5) : () ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () (i) ; (ii) , ; (iii) ; (iv) ; (v) ; ? () , ? , : () , ? () 2000 , , , , , ? () (i) , , ,

(ii) , (iii) ? () (i) , (ii) , , (iii) , (iv) , (v) ? () , ? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provin-cial Councils : (a) Will he inform this House in detail, the procedure followed by the Road Passenger Transport Author-ity of Southern Province when issuing licences for buses for passenger transport services? (b) Will he submit to this House separately, the num-ber of passenger transport service licences issued by the said Authority since the year 2000 up to now along with the names of the licensees, their addresses, the registered numbers of those buses, the relevant routes, the dates of application for licences and the dates on which licences were is-sued? (c) Will he state separately, (i) if routes have been revised out of those the names of the licensees concerned, their ad-dresses and the registered numbers of the buses; (ii) the former routes and the revised routes; and, (iii) the dates of application for revision and the dates revisions were issued? (d) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of those who have applied for route revisions but not granted so far; (ii) their names, addresses and the dates of applica-tion for licences; (iii) the reasons for not granting the said revisions; (iv) whether approval will be granted for those in future; and, (v) for which licences? (e) If not, why?

2008 04 2411 2412

( ) (The Hon. Janaka Bandara Thennakoon) () . . () . 496. ( 01 .) () (i) 2000 02 . (ii) 02 . (iii) 02 . . () (i) . . . (ii) . (iii) . (iv) . ( .) . (v) () . () .

()

496 ( . 01 .) () (i) 2000 . 02 . (ii) . 02 . (iii) . 02 . . () (i) , . , . . (ii) (iii) . (iv) . ( ) . v. , () (a) Yes. Tenders will be called for the provision of Identi-fied services by the notices published in the news-papers and new licences for passenger transport will be issued based on the selection of bidders who have submitted the maximum bid for each service. 18 PL 002931 (2008/04)

2413 2414

(b) Yes. Number of licences are 496. (other details have been tabled under Annex-01). (c) (i) Particulars of route revisions made with regard to services in operation at present under the licences issued from 2000 to date have been tabled under Annex-02. (ii) tabled under Annex-02. (iii) Date of route revisions effected is submitted under Annex-02. However, since date of appli-cation has not been registered it is difficult to provide an exact date. (d) (i) Route revisions have been granted considering practicability and the routes where services are required, without any delay. However, some requests for route revisions, if granted may cause hindrance to the existing time table or an injustice to other investors in connection with requirement of services in operation, have not been granted and removed. Since such particu-lars have not been written down, the amount has not been given.

(ii) Unable to give as per above answer. (iii) Under the route revisions requested some re-quests are rejected based on causing an injus-tice to present licencees or requirement of the service of respective applicant or completion of the time table of respective route or issues which affect other services in the respective route. (iv) Action will not be taken with regard to applica-tions for route revisions which have been iden-tified as unable to be granted by the Authority in terms of its criteria. (More issues may arise as they were forwarded before a long period). However, if re-requests are made for route re-visions the possibility of granting same will be considered based on present requirement of the service and they may be granted. (v) For specifically identified licences in terms of the aforesaid criteria of the Authority for future route revisions. (e) Not applicable.

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue, Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.
